RACE OVERVIEW
=============
The 2024 Formula 1 Canadian Grand Prix was a thrilling race held at the Circuit Gilles Villeneuve, characterized by mixed weather conditions. Max Verstappen of Red Bull emerged victorious, overcoming rain showers, multiple safety car periods, and a strong challenge from Lando Norris of McLaren. George Russell initially started on pole, but Verstappen ultimately took the lead and held on to win. The race saw several key moments, including a safety car caused by Logan Sargeant's crash, and strategic gambles with tire choices due to the changing weather. Several drivers retired due to incidents or mechanical issues, including Charles LeClerc and Sergio Perez.
